PUBLIC NOTICE
I, R. Rose Mary daughter of Thiru M. Ramu aged 29 years, residing at 19/4, Padavettamman Koil Street,
Asthinapuram, Kannivakkam Post, Guduvancherry (Via) Kancheepuram District, wish to state that, I am Married to
Mr. D. Pushparaj son of Thiru A Dhanaraj on 11th May 2016 which was duly registered, before Marriage Registrar,
Chengalpattu, (M.I. No. 18/2016) dated 31st May 2016.
At the time of my Marriage with Mr. Pushparaj, he had a boy child named Jebaraj. P. born on 9th November 2010
(Birth Certificate Reg. No. 2010/06/86A/007054 dated 11th November 2010) to his first wife Mrs. Gnanamary, daughter of
Thiru M. Ramu, (My own Sister), She Died on 19th January 2015 Death Certificate No. 01/2015, dated 2nd Februay 2015)
By Virtue of my Marriage with Mr. Pushparaj. D, I have become the step Mother of Jebaraj. P. This Public notice
is being issued by me whole heartedly, on my own willing without any Prejudice/Coersion.
Chennai,
3rd July 2017.

R. ROSE MARY
(Step Mother)

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
